    private void jButton1ActionPerformed(ActionEvent evt)
    {
        String PIDCheck = jTextField3.getText();
        int check = PIDCheck.length();
        if(check == 0)
            jTextField3.setText("0");
        int pkmnPIDs = DatatypeConverter.parseInt(jTextField3.getText());
        long pkmnPID = getUnsignedInt(pkmnPIDs);
        String partyEXP = "";
        String partyStat = "";
        String partyTrainer = "";
        String shadowpartyAddress = "";
        String shadowpartyValue = "";
        String partyLV = "";
        String partyPID = "";
        String partySpecies = "";
        String pkmnID = "";
        String partyEV = "";
        String partySID = "";
        String partyNick = "";
        String partymove1 = "";
        String partymove2 = "";
        String partymove3 = "";
        String partymove4 = "";
        String pkmnmove1 = "";
        String pkmnmove2 = "";
        String pkmnmove3 = "";
        String pkmnmove4 = "";
        String partyslotsel = "";
        int ShadowCombo = jComboBox4.getSelectedIndex();
        int PartyCombo = jComboBox3.getSelectedIndex();

    public static void main(String args[])
        throws FileNotFoundException
    {
        try
        {
            javax.swing.UIManager.LookAndFeelInfo alookandfeelinfo[] = UIManager.getInstalledLookAndFeels();
            int i = alookandfeelinfo.length;
            int j = 0;
            do
            {
                if(j >= i)
                    break;
                javax.swing.UIManager.LookAndFeelInfo info = alookandfeelinfo[j];
                if("Nimbus".equals(info.getName()))
                {
                    UIManager.setLookAndFeel(info.getClassName());
                    break;
                }
                j++;
            } while(true);
        }
        catch(Exception ex)
        {
            Logger.getLogger(my/contacteditor/ContactEditorUI.getName()).log(Level.SEVERE, null, ex);
        }
        PrintStream console = System.out;
        File file = new File("C:\\cheats\\Pokemon XD.txt");
        try
        {
            PrintStream ps = new PrintStream(file);
            System.setOut(ps);
        }
        catch(IOException e) { }
        EventQueue.invokeLater(new  Object()     /* anonymous class not found */
    class _anm8 {}

);
    }

    public static long getUnsignedInt(int number)
    {
        return (long)number & 0xffffffffL;
    }
